trīṇi aśītim ca bhokṣyanti vasudhām śakāḥ mā aśītī dve ca varṣāṇi bhoktāraḥ yavanāḥ mahīm pañca varṣa śatāni iha tuṣārāṇām mahī smṛtā jātayaḥ śatāni trīṇi bhokṣyante maunāḥ ekādaśa eva tu teṣu chinneṣu kālena tatas kilakilaḥ nṛpaḥ samāḥ ṣaṇṇavatim ca eva pṛthivīm tu sameṣyati nṛpān vaidiśakān ca atha bhaviṣyān tu nibodhata śeṣasya nāga rājasya putraḥ sura purañjayaḥ bhogī bhaviṣyate rājā nṛpaḥ nāga kula udvahaḥ sadācandraḥ tu candrāśuḥ dvitīyaḥ nakhavant tathā dhanadharmā tatas ca api caturthaḥ vaṃśa jaḥ smṛtaḥ tasya bhrātā yavīyāḥ tu nāmnā nandiyaśāḥ kila daihitraḥ śiśikaḥ nāma pūrikāyām nṛpaḥ abhavat vindhyaśakti sutaḥ ca api pravīraḥ nāma vīryavān bhokṣyate ca samāḥ ṣaṣṭim purīm kāñcanakām ca vai yakṣyate vājapeyaiḥ ca samāpta vara dakṣiṇaiḥ vindhyakānām kulānām te nṛpāḥ vaivāhikāḥ trayaḥ supratīkaḥ gabhīraḥ ca samāḥ bhokṣyati viṃśatim śaṅkamānaḥ abhavat rājā mahiṣīṇām mahīpatiḥ puṣpa mitrāḥ bhaviṣyanti ṣaṭ stri mitrāḥ trayodaśa mekalāyām nṛpāḥ sapta bhaviṣyanti ca saptatiḥ tu rājānaḥ bhaviṣyanti mahā balāḥ naiṣadhāḥ pārthivāḥ sarve bhaviṣyatyām anu kṣayāt nala vaṃśa prasūtāḥ te vīryavantaḥ mahā balāḥ magadhānām mahā vīryaḥ viśvasphāṇiḥ bhaviṣyati utsādya pārthivān sarvān saḥ anyān varṇān kariṣyati kaivartān madrakān ca iva pulindān brāhmaṇān tathā sthāpayiṣyanti nānā deśeṣu te janān viśva sphāṇiḥ mahā sattvaḥ yuddhe viṣṇu sama prabhaḥ viśva sphāṇiḥ narapatiḥ klība ākṛtiḥ iva ucyate nava nāgāḥ tu bhokṣyati purīm caṃpāvatīm nṛpāḥ mathurām ca purā ramyām nāgāḥ bhokṣyanti sapta vai anu gaṅgā prayāgam ca sāketam magadhān tathā etān janapadān sarvān bhokṣyante sapta vaṃśa jāḥ na eṣa dhānya dukān ca eva śaiśītān kālatoyakān etān janapadān sarvān bhokṣyante maṇidhānya jān kośalān ca āndhrapaiṇḍrān ca tāmraliptān sa sāgarān campām ca eva purīm ramyām bhokṣyante deva rakṣitāḥ kaliṅgāḥ mahiṣāḥ ca eva mahendra nilayāḥ ca ye etān janapadān sarvān pālayiṣyati vai guhaḥ strī rāṣṭra bhojakān ca eva bhokṣyate kanakāhvayaḥ alpa prasādāḥ hi anṛtāḥ mahā krodhāḥ hi adhārmikāḥ na eva mūrddhābhiṣiktāḥ te bhaviṣyanti narādhipāḥ yuga doṣa durācārāḥ bhaviṣyanti nṛpāḥ tu te bhaviṣyanti iha payāye kālena vṛthivīkṣitaḥ taiḥ vimiśrāḥ janapadāḥ mleccha ācārāḥ ca sarvaśas viparyayeṇa vartante na āśāyiṣyanti vai prajāḥ lubdhāḥ anṛta vācaḥ ca bhavitāraḥ tadā nṛpāḥ teṣām varttati paryāye bahustrīke yuge tadā lavāt lavam bhraśyamānāḥ āyu rūpa bala śrutaiḥ tathā gatāsu vai kāṣṭham prajāsu jagatī īśvarāḥ rājānaḥ saṃpraṇaśyati kālena upahatāḥ tadā kalkinā vyāhatāḥ sarve mlecchāḥ yāsyanti saṃkṣayam adhārmikāḥ ca ye atyartham pākhaṇḍāḥ ca eva sarvaśas pranaṣṭe nṛpa śabde ca saṃdhyā śiṣṭe kalau yuge kiñcid śiṣṭāḥ prajāḥ tāḥ vai dharme naṣṭe parigrahāḥ asādhanāḥ hata svāḥ ca vyādhi śoka nipīḍitāḥ anāvṛṣṭi hatāḥ ca eva paraspara vadhena ca anādhārāḥ paritrastāḥ vārtām utsṛjya duḥkhitāḥ tyaktvā purāṇi grāmān ca bhaviṣyanti vanaukasaḥ evaṃrūpeṣu naṣṭeṣu prajāḥ tyaktvā gṛhāṇi tu naṣṭe snehe durāpannāḥ bhraṣṭa snehāḥ suhṛd janaḥ varṇa āśrama paribhraṣṭāḥ saṃkaram ghoram āsthitāḥ saritaḥ sāgara anūpān sevante parvatān atha aṅgān kaliṅgān vaṅgān ca kāśmīrān kāśi kośalān mānavāḥ kṛtsnam himavataḥ pṛṣṭham kūlam ca lavaṇāmbhasaḥ mṛgaiḥ mīnaiḥ vihaṃgaiḥ ca śvāpadaiḥ ca ikṣubhiḥ tathā madhu śāka phalaiḥ mūlaiḥ vartayiṣyanti mānavāḥ cīram parṇam ca vividham valkalāni ajināni ca bīja annāni tathā hantaḥ kāṣṭha śaṅkubhiḥ aja eḍakam khara uṣṭram ca pālayiṣyanti yatnatas nadīḥ vatsyanti toya arthe nūnam āśritya mānavāḥ bahu manyāḥ prajā hīnāḥ śauca ācāra vivarjitāḥ hīnān dīnān tathā adharmān prajā samanuvartsyati durbalāḥ viṣaya glānāḥ jarayā saṃpariplutāḥ patra mūla phala āhārāḥ cīra kṛṣṇa ajina ambarāḥ etad kālam anuprāptāḥ prajāḥ kali yuga antake niḥśeṣāḥ tu bhaviṣyanti sārdham kali yugena tu sa saṃdhyāṃśe tu niḥśeṣe kṛtam vai pratipatsyate yadā yandraḥ ca sūryaḥ ca tathā tiṣya bṛhaspatī eka rāśau bhaviṣyanti tadā kṛta yugam bhavet eṣa vaṃśa kramaḥ kṛtsnaḥ kīrtitaḥ vaḥ yathākramam atītāḥ vartamānāḥ ca tathā eva anāgatāḥ ca ye mahānanda abhiṣeka anta janma yāvat parīkṣitaḥ etat varṣa sahasram tu jñeyam pañcāśat uttaram pramāṇam vai tathā vaktum mahāpadma uttaram ca yat antaram ca śatāni aṣṭau ṣaṭtriṃśat ca samāḥ smṛtāḥ etad kāla antara bhāvya mandhra anta ādyāḥ prakīrttitāḥ bhaviṣyaiḥ tatra saṃkhyātāḥ purāṇa jñaiḥ śruta ṛṣibhiḥ saptarṣayaḥ tadā prāptāḥ pitrye pārīkṣite śatam saptaviṃśaiḥ śataiḥ bhāvyāḥ andhrāṇām te anvayāḥ punar saptarṣayaḥ tu tiṣṭhanti paryāyeṇa śatam śatam saptarṣīṇām yugam tu etat divyayā saṃkhyayā smṛtam māsāḥ divyāḥ smṛtāḥ ṣaṭ ca divya abdāḥ ca eva sapta hi saptarṣīṇām tu yau pūrvau dṛśyete uttarā diśi tena saptarṣayaḥ yuktāḥ jñeyāḥ vyomni śatam samāḥ nakṣatrāṇām ṛṣīṇām ca bhogasya etat nidarśanam saptarṣayaḥ hi atha a yuktāḥ kāle parīkṣite śatam andhra aṃśe sa caturviṃśe bhaviṣyanti śatam samāḥ imāḥ tadā tu prakṛtīḥ vyāpatsyante prajāḥ bhṛśam anṛta upahatāḥ sarvāḥ dharmataḥ kāmataḥ ṛthataḥ śrauta smārte praśithile dharme varṇa āśrame tadā saṃkaram durbala ātmānaḥ pratiyāsyanti mohitāḥ saṃsaktāḥ ca bhaviṣyanti śūdrāḥ sārdham dvijātibhiḥ brāhmaṇāḥ śūdra yaṣṭāraḥ śūdrāḥ vai mantra yonayaḥ upasthāsyanti tān viprān tadā daurvṛttya lipsavaḥ lavāt lavam bhraśyamānāḥ prajāḥ sarvāḥ krameṇa tu kṣayam eva gamiṣyanti kṣīṇa śeṣāḥ yuga kṣaye yasmin kṛṣṇaḥ divyam yātaḥ tasmin eva tadā dine sahasrāṇām śatāni iha trīṇi mānuṣa saṃkhyayā tu ucyate kaliḥ divyam varṣa sahasram tu tat saṃdhyāṃśe hi kīrtite niḥśeṣe ca tadā tasmin kṛtam vai pratipatsyate a ilaḥ ca ikṣvāku vaṃśaḥ ca saha bhedaiḥ prakīrtitau tu samṛtam kṣatram sumitrā antam vivasvantaḥ ailam kṣatram kṣemakāntam soma vaṃśa vidaḥ viduḥ ete vivasvantaḥ putrāḥ kīrtitāḥ kīrti vardhanāḥ atītāḥ vartamānāḥ ca tathā eva anāgatāḥ ca ye brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyaḥ śūdrāḥ ca eva atra ye smṛtāḥ yuge yuge mahātmānaḥ samatītāḥ sahasraśas bahu tvāt nāmadheyānām parisaṃkhyā kulekule etasyām tu yuga ākhyāyām yatas kṣattram prapatsyate devāpiḥ pauravaḥ rājā aikṣvākuḥ ca eva yaḥ maruḥ navaviṃśe yuge saḥ atha vaṃśasya ādiḥ bhaviṣyati devāpeḥ ca sa paulaḥ tu elādiḥ bhavitā nṛpaḥ evam sarvatra vijñeyam saṃtāna arthe tu latraṇam gotrāṇām kṣatriyāṇām ca bhaviṣyete pravartakau dvāpara aṃśena tiṣṭhanti kṣatriyāḥ ṛṣibhiḥ saha evam eva tu sarveṣu tiṣṭhanti iha asureṣu vai saptarṣayaḥ nṛpaiḥ sārdham saṃtāna artham yuge yuge manvantarāṇām saptānām saṃtānaḥ ca śrutaḥ ca te yathā pravṛttiḥ teṣām vai pravṛttānām tathā kṣayaḥ saptarṣayaḥ viduḥ teṣām dīrgha āyuḥ tvāt bhava abhavau utpadyamānāḥ tretāyām kṣīyamāṇāḥ kalau punar anuyānti yuga ākhyām tu yāvat manvantara kṣayaḥ jāmadagnyena rāmeṇa kṣatre niravaśeṣite kṛtā iyam saṃkulā sarvā kṣatriyaiḥ vasudhādhipaiḥ dvi paṃśa kāraṇam ca eva kīrtayiṣye nibodhata rājānaḥ śreṇi baddhāḥ tu tathā anye kṣatriyāḥ nṛpāḥ ye khyātāḥ tathā eva ikṣvākavaḥ nṛpāḥ teṣām eka śatam pūrṇam kulānām abhiṣekitam tāvat eva tu bhojānām vistaraḥ dviguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ bhajate tri aṃśakam kṣattram dyathā diśam teṣu atītāḥ samānāḥ ye bruvataḥ tān nibodhata śatam vai prativindhyānām śatam nāgāḥ sa haihayāḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ ca ekaśatam aśītiḥ janamejayāḥ śatam ca brahmadattānām śāriṇām viriṇām śatam tatas śatam tu paulānām śveta kāśya kuśa ādayaḥ tatas apare sahasram vai ye atītāḥ śaśavindavaḥ yajire ca aśvamedhaiḥ te sarve niyuta dakṣiṇaiḥ evam rājarṣayaḥ atītā śataśas atha sahasraśas teṣām nibodhata utpannāḥ loke saṃtatayaḥ smṛtāḥ na śakye vistaraḥ tāsām saṃtatīnām parasparam aṣṭāviṃśat yuga ākhyāḥ tu gatāḥ vaivasvata intare etaiḥ rājarṣibhiḥ sārdham śaṣṭāyāḥ tāḥ nibodhata catvāriṃśat trayaḥ ca eva bhaviṣyāḥ saha rājbhiḥ śiṣṭāḥ tu tatas vaivasvata kṣayaḥ ete yayāti putrāṇām pañca vaṃśāḥ viśām hitāḥ kīrttitāḥ ca vyatītāḥ ye ye lokān dhārayanti uta āyuḥ kīrtim dhanam putrān svargam ca ānantyam aśnute dhāraṇāt śravaṇāt ca eva pañcavaṃśasya dhīmataḥ iti eṣa vaḥ mayā pādaḥ tṛtīyaḥ kathitaḥ dvijāḥ vistareṇa ānupūrvyā ca kim bhūyas varṇayāmi aham iti śrī brahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyu prokte madhyama bhāge tṛtīye upoddhāta pāde vaṃśānuvarṇanam nāma catuḥsaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ ca ayam tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ
